# Allows you to create your own dynamic keys
# to be called in localization.
# defined_text -> this is it, we're defining the text
# text -> a discrete entry that can be picked to display in loc.
# trigger -> determines if a text entry will be picked or not.
# (The triggers need to be valid for the scope the key is called in
# (eg Root or From.From).)
# localization_key -> points to the localization key
# that'll be used if trigger passes

defined_text = {
    name = GetEnableAutoBuildTitle
    text = {
        trigger = { 
          has_global_flag = autobuild_flag
        }
        localization_key = "autobuild_enabled_loc"
    }
	text = {
		localization_key = "autobuild_disabled_loc"
	}
}
defined_text = {
    name = GetGDPAmount
    text = {
        trigger = { 
            set_temp_variable = { gdp_amount_temp = gdp_amount }
			check_variable = { gdp_amount_temp < 1000 }
        }
        localization_key = "[?gdp_amount_temp]"
    }
	text = {
        trigger = { 
            divide_temp_variable = { gdp_amount_temp = 1000 }
		}
        localization_key = "[?gdp_amount_temp]K"
    }
}
defined_text = {
    name = GetYearlyGDPAmount
    text = {
        trigger = { 
            set_temp_variable = { gdp_amount_temp = gdp_amount }
			check_variable = { gdp_amount_temp > 83333.333 }
            divide_temp_variable = { gdp_amount_temp = 1000000 }
			multiply_temp_variable = { gdp_amount_temp = 12 }
        }
        localization_key = "[?gdp_amount_temp]M"
    }
	text = {
        trigger = { 
            set_temp_variable = { gdp_amount_temp = gdp_amount }
			check_variable = { gdp_amount_temp > 83.333 }
            divide_temp_variable = { gdp_amount_temp = 1000 }
			multiply_temp_variable = { gdp_amount_temp = 12 }
		}
        localization_key = "[?gdp_amount_temp]K"
    }
	text = {
        trigger = { 
            set_temp_variable = { gdp_amount_temp = gdp_amount }
			multiply_temp_variable = { gdp_amount_temp = 12 }
		}
        localization_key = "[?gdp_amount_temp]"
    }
}
# General
	defined_text = { # GetAdjustedAmount
		name = GetAdjustedAmount
		text = {
			trigger = {
				check_variable = { amount_temp = 0 }
			}
			localization_key = "[?amount_temp|=1]"
		}
		text = {
			trigger = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = { amount_temp > 99999.999 }
					check_variable = { amount_temp < -99999.999 }
				}
				set_temp_variable = { number_temp = amount_temp }
				divide_temp_variable = { number_temp = 1000 }
			}
			localization_key = "[?number_temp|=0]K"
		}
		text = {
			trigger = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = { amount_temp > 9999.999 }
					check_variable = { amount_temp < -9999.999 }
				}
				set_temp_variable = { number_temp = amount_temp }
				divide_temp_variable = { number_temp = 1000 }
			}
			localization_key = "[?number_temp|=1]K"
		}
		text = {
			trigger = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = { amount_temp > 999.999 }
					check_variable = { amount_temp < -999.999 }
				}
				set_temp_variable = { number_temp = amount_temp }
				divide_temp_variable = { number_temp = 1000 }
			}
			localization_key = "[?number_temp|=2]K"
		}
		text = {
			trigger = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = { amount_temp > 99.999 }
					check_variable = { amount_temp < -99.999 }
				}
			}
			localization_key = "[?amount_temp|=0]"
		}
		text = {
			trigger = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = { amount_temp > 9.999 }
					check_variable = { amount_temp < -9.999 }
				}
			}
			localization_key = "[?amount_temp|=1]"
		}
		text = {
			trigger = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = { amount_temp > 0.999 }
					check_variable = { amount_temp < -0.999 }
				}
			}
			localization_key = "[?amount_temp|=2]"
		}
		text = {
			localization_key = "[?amount_temp|=3]"
		}
	}
	defined_text = { # GetPositiveColor
		name = GetPositiveColor
		text = {
			trigger = {
				check_variable = { amount_temp > 0 }
			}
			localization_key = green_loc
		}
		text = {
			trigger = {
				check_variable = { amount_temp < 0 }
			}
			localization_key = red_loc
		}
		text = {
			localization_key = yellow_loc
		}
	}
	defined_text = { # GetPositiveAdjustedAmount
		name = GetPositiveAdjustedAmount
		text = {
			localization_key = "[GetPositiveColor][GetAdjustedAmount]"
		}
	}

#Pie Chart
    defined_text = {
        name = GetValueToPopType
        text = {
            trigger = {
                state = 1
            }

			defined_text = {
				name = GetBuildingBasicProfit
				text = {
					trigger = {
						set_temp_variable = { bld_tkn = v }
						set_temp_variable = { bld_o1 = global.building_output_resource_1@var:bld_tkn }
						set_temp_variable = { bld_o2 = global.building_output_resource_2@var:bld_tkn }
						set_temp_variable = { bld_o3 = global.building_output_resource_3@var:bld_tkn }
						set_temp_variable = { bld_o4 = global.building_output_resource_4@var:bld_tkn }
						set_temp_variable = { bld_o5 = global.building_output_resource_5@var:bld_tkn }

						set_temp_variable = { output_modifier_temp = building_output_factor@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { output_modifier_temp = 1 }

						set_temp_variable = { throughput_modifier_temp = building_throughput_factor@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { throughput_modifier_temp = 1 }

						set_temp_variable = { input_modifier_temp = building_input_factor@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { input_modifier_temp = 1 }

						set_temp_variable = { size_modifier_temp = building_size_factor@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { size_modifier_temp = 1 }

						#Revenue
						set_temp_variable = { gip_profit = price@var:bld_o1 }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_profit = global.building_basic_output_1@var:bld_tkn }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_profit = size@var:bld_tkn }
						
						set_temp_variable = { gip_temp = price@var:bld_o2 }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_temp = global.building_basic_output_2@var:bld_tkn }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_temp = size@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { gip_profit = gip_temp }
						
						set_temp_variable = { gip_temp = price@var:bld_o3 }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_temp = global.building_basic_output_3@var:bld_tkn }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_temp = size@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { gip_profit = gip_temp }
						
						set_temp_variable = { gip_temp = price@var:bld_o4 }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_temp = global.building_basic_output_4@var:bld_tkn }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_temp = size@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { gip_profit = gip_temp }
						
						set_temp_variable = { gip_temp = price@var:bld_o5 }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_temp = global.building_basic_output_5@var:bld_tkn }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_temp = size@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { gip_profit = gip_temp }
						
						set_temp_variable = { gip_temp = price_industrial_capacity }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_temp = global.building_basic_output_industrial_capacity@var:bld_tkn }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_temp = size@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { gip_profit = gip_temp }

						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_profit = output_modifier_temp }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_profit = throughput_modifier_temp }

						#Expenses
						set_temp_variable = { gip_exp = global.building_industrial_capacity_use@var:bld_tkn }
						set_temp_variable = { cap_modifier_temp = building_industrial_capacity_use_factor@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { cap_modifier_temp = 1 }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = size@var:bld_tkn }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = cap_modifier_temp }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = input_modifier_temp }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = throughput_modifier_temp }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = price_industrial_capacity }
						subtract_from_temp_variable = { gip_profit = gip_exp }
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { global.building_basic_input_amount_1@var:bld_tkn > 0 }
							}
							set_temp_variable = { gip_imr = global.building_basic_input_resource_1@var:bld_tkn }

							set_temp_variable = { gip_exp = global.building_basic_input_amount_1@var:bld_tkn }
							multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = price@var:gip_imr }
							multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = input_modifier_temp }
							multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = throughput_modifier_temp }
							multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = size@var:bld_tkn }
							subtract_from_temp_variable = { gip_profit = gip_exp }
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { global.building_basic_input_amount_2@var:bld_tkn > 0 }
							}
							set_temp_variable = { gip_imr = global.building_basic_input_resource_2@var:bld_tkn }

							set_temp_variable = { gip_exp = global.building_basic_input_amount_2@var:bld_tkn }
							multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = price@var:gip_imr }
							multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = input_modifier_temp }
							multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = throughput_modifier_temp }
							multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = size@var:bld_tkn }
							subtract_from_temp_variable = { gip_profit = gip_exp }
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { global.building_basic_input_amount_3@var:bld_tkn > 0 }
							}
							set_temp_variable = { gip_imr = global.building_basic_input_resource_3@var:bld_tkn }

						set_temp_variable = { bld_o1 = global.building_output_resource_1@var:bld_tkn }
						set_temp_variable = { bld_o2 = global.building_output_resource_2@var:bld_tkn }
						set_temp_variable = { bld_o3 = global.building_output_resource_3@var:bld_tkn }
						set_temp_variable = { bld_o4 = global.building_output_resource_4@var:bld_tkn }
						set_temp_variable = { bld_o5 = global.building_output_resource_5@var:bld_tkn }

						set_temp_variable = { output_modifier_temp = building_output_factor@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { output_modifier_temp = 1 }

						set_temp_variable = { throughput_modifier_temp = building_throughput_factor@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { throughput_modifier_temp = 1 }

						set_temp_variable = { input_modifier_temp = building_input_factor@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { input_modifier_temp = 1 }

						set_temp_variable = { size_modifier_temp = building_size_factor@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { size_modifier_temp = 1 }

						#Revenue
						set_temp_variable = { gip_profit = price@var:bld_o1 }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_profit = global.building_basic_output_1@var:bld_tkn }
						
						set_temp_variable = { gip_temp = price@var:bld_o2 }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_temp = global.building_basic_output_2@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { gip_profit = gip_temp }
						
						set_temp_variable = { gip_temp = price@var:bld_o3 }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_temp = global.building_basic_output_3@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { gip_profit = gip_temp }
						
						set_temp_variable = { gip_temp = price@var:bld_o4 }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_temp = global.building_basic_output_4@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { gip_profit = gip_temp }
						
						set_temp_variable = { gip_temp = price@var:bld_o5 }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_temp = global.building_basic_output_5@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { gip_profit = gip_temp }
						
						set_temp_variable = { gip_temp = price_industrial_capacity }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_temp = global.building_basic_output_industrial_capacity@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { gip_profit = gip_temp }

						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_profit = output_modifier_temp }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_profit = throughput_modifier_temp }

						#Expenses
						set_temp_variable = { gip_exp = global.building_industrial_capacity_use@var:bld_tkn }
						set_temp_variable = { cap_modifier_temp = building_industrial_capacity_use_factor@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { cap_modifier_temp = 1 }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = cap_modifier_temp }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = input_modifier_temp }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = throughput_modifier_temp }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = price_industrial_capacity }
						subtract_from_temp_variable = { gip_profit = gip_exp }

						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { global.building_basic_input_amount_1@var:bld_tkn > 0 }
							}
							set_temp_variable = { gip_imr = global.building_basic_input_resource_1@var:bld_tkn }

							set_temp_variable = { gip_exp = global.building_basic_input_amount_1@var:bld_tkn }
							multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = price@var:gip_imr }
							multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = input_modifier_temp }
							multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = throughput_modifier_temp }
							subtract_from_temp_variable = { gip_profit = gip_exp }
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { global.building_basic_input_amount_2@var:bld_tkn > 0 }
							}
							set_temp_variable = { gip_imr = global.building_basic_input_resource_2@var:bld_tkn }

							set_temp_variable = { gip_exp = global.building_basic_input_amount_2@var:bld_tkn }
							multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = price@var:gip_imr }
							multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = input_modifier_temp }
							multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = throughput_modifier_temp }
							subtract_from_temp_variable = { gip_profit = gip_exp }
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { global.building_basic_input_amount_3@var:bld_tkn > 0 }
							}
							set_temp_variable = { gip_imr = global.building_basic_input_resource_3@var:bld_tkn }

							set_temp_variable = { gip_exp = global.building_basic_input_amount_3@var:bld_tkn }
							multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = price@var:gip_imr }
							multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = input_modifier_temp }
							multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = throughput_modifier_temp }
							subtract_from_temp_variable = { gip_profit = gip_exp }

							limit = {
								check_variable = { global.building_basic_input_amount_4@var:bld_tkn > 0 }
							}
							set_temp_variable = { gip_imr = global.building_basic_input_resource_4@var:bld_tkn }

							set_temp_variable = { gip_exp = global.building_basic_input_amount_4@var:bld_tkn }

							multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = throughput_modifier_temp }
							subtract_from_temp_variable = { gip_profit = gip_exp }

								check_variable = { global.building_basic_input_amount_5@var:bld_tkn > 0 }
							}
							set_temp_variable = { gip_imr = global.building_basic_input_resource_5@var:bld_tkn }

							set_temp_variable = { gip_exp = global.building_basic_input_amount_5@var:bld_tkn }
							multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = price@var:gip_imr }
							multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = input_modifier_temp }
							multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = throughput_modifier_temp }
							subtract_from_temp_variable = { gip_profit = gip_exp }

						set_temp_variable = { gip_employees = global.building_basic_peasants_employment@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { gip_employees = global.building_basic_laborers_employment@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { gip_employees = global.building_basic_workers_employment@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { gip_employees = global.building_basic_professionals_employment@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { gip_employees = global.building_basic_specialists_employment@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { gip_employees = global.building_basic_aristocrats_employment@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { gip_employees = global.building_basic_capitalists_employment@var:bld_tkn }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_employees = size_modifier_temp }

						divide_temp_variable = { gip_profit = gip_employees }

						set_temp_variable = { avg_wage_temp = 0 }
						set_temp_variable = { gip_exp = global.building_basic_peasants_employment@var:bld_tkn }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = 1 }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = size_modifier_temp }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = base_wage@var:bld_tkn }

						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = 2 }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = size_modifier_temp }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = base_wage@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { avg_wage_temp = gip_exp }

						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = 5 }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = size_modifier_temp }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = base_wage@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { avg_wage_temp = gip_exp }

						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = 10 }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = size_modifier_temp }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = base_wage@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { avg_wage_temp = gip_exp }
						
						set_temp_variable = { gip_exp = global.building_basic_specialists_employment@var:bld_tkn }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = 20 }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = size_modifier_temp }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = base_wage@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { avg_wage_temp = gip_exp }
						
						set_temp_variable = { gip_exp = global.building_basic_aristocrats_employment@var:bld_tkn }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = 30 }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = size_modifier_temp }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = base_wage@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { avg_wage_temp = gip_exp }
						
						set_temp_variable = { gip_exp = global.building_basic_capitalists_employment@var:bld_tkn }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = 50 }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = size_modifier_temp }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = base_wage@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { avg_wage_temp = gip_exp }

						divide_temp_variable = { avg_wage_temp = gip_employees }
						check_variable = { avg_wage_temp < gip_profit }
					}
					localization_key = "[?gip_profit|3G]"
				}
				text = {
					trigger = {
						check_variable = { avg_wage_temp > gip_profit }
					}
					localization_key = "[?gip_profit|3R]"
				}
				text = {
					localization_key = "[?gip_profit|3Y]"
				}

		#Advanced
			defined_text = {
				name = GetBuildingAdvancedPrerequisites
				text = {
					trigger = {
						set_temp_variable = { gicc = v }
						set_temp_variable = { gicct = global.building_advanced_tech_unlock@var:gicc }
						check_variable = { gicct = 0 }
					}
					localization_key = "building_pm_advanced_never_tt"
				}
				text = {
					trigger = {
						check_variable = { gicct = 1 }
					}
					localization_key = ""
				}
				text = {
					trigger = {
						controller = { has_tech = var:gicct }
					}
					localization_key = "building_pm_advanced_tech_yes_tt"
				}
				text = {
					localization_key = "building_pm_advanced_tech_no_tt"
				}
			}
			defined_text = {
				name = GetBuildingAdvancedTech
				text = {
					trigger = {
						set_temp_variable = { bld_tkn = v }
						set_temp_variable = { bld_tmp = global.building_advanced_tech_unlock@var:bld_tkn }
					}
					localization_key = "[?bld_tmp.GetTokenLocalizedKey]"
				}
			}
			defined_text = {
				name = GetBuildingAdvancedProfit
				text = {
					trigger = {
						set_temp_variable = { bld_tkn = v }
						set_temp_variable = { bld_o1 = global.building_output_resource_1@var:bld_tkn }
						set_temp_variable = { bld_o2 = global.building_output_resource_2@var:bld_tkn }
						set_temp_variable = { bld_o3 = global.building_output_resource_3@var:bld_tkn }
						set_temp_variable = { bld_o4 = global.building_output_resource_4@var:bld_tkn }
						set_temp_variable = { bld_o5 = global.building_output_resource_5@var:bld_tkn }

						set_temp_variable = { output_modifier_temp = building_output_factor@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { output_modifier_temp = 1 }

						set_temp_variable = { throughput_modifier_temp = building_throughput_factor@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { throughput_modifier_temp = 1 }

						set_temp_variable = { input_modifier_temp = building_input_factor@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { input_modifier_temp = 1 }

						set_temp_variable = { size_modifier_temp = building_size_factor@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { size_modifier_temp = 1 }

						#Revenue
						set_temp_variable = { gip_profit = price@var:bld_o1 }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_profit = global.building_advanced_output_1@var:bld_tkn }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_profit = size@var:bld_tkn }
						
						set_temp_variable = { gip_temp = price@var:bld_o2 }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_temp = global.building_advanced_output_2@var:bld_tkn }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_temp = size@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { gip_profit = gip_temp }
						
						set_temp_variable = { gip_temp = price@var:bld_o3 }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_temp = global.building_advanced_output_3@var:bld_tkn }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_temp = size@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { gip_profit = gip_temp }
						
						set_temp_variable = { gip_temp = price@var:bld_o4 }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_temp = global.building_advanced_output_4@var:bld_tkn }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_temp = size@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { gip_profit = gip_temp }
						
						set_temp_variable = { gip_temp = price@var:bld_o5 }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_temp = global.building_advanced_output_5@var:bld_tkn }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_temp = size@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { gip_profit = gip_temp }
						
						set_temp_variable = { gip_temp = price_industrial_capacity }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_temp = global.building_advanced_output_industrial_capacity@var:bld_tkn }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_temp = size@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { gip_profit = gip_temp }

						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_profit = output_modifier_temp }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_profit = throughput_modifier_temp }

						#Expenses
						set_temp_variable = { gip_exp = global.building_industrial_capacity_use@var:bld_tkn }
						set_temp_variable = { cap_modifier_temp = building_industrial_capacity_use_factor@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { cap_modifier_temp = 1 }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = size@var:bld_tkn }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = cap_modifier_temp }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = input_modifier_temp }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = throughput_modifier_temp }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = price_industrial_capacity }
						subtract_from_temp_variable = { gip_profit = gip_exp }
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { global.building_advanced_input_amount_1@var:bld_tkn > 0 }
							}
							set_temp_variable = { gip_imr = global.building_advanced_input_resource_1@var:bld_tkn }

							set_temp_variable = { gip_exp = global.building_advanced_input_amount_1@var:bld_tkn }
							multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = price@var:gip_imr }
							multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = input_modifier_temp }
							multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = throughput_modifier_temp }
							multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = size@var:bld_tkn }
							subtract_from_temp_variable = { gip_profit = gip_exp }
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { global.building_advanced_input_amount_2@var:bld_tkn > 0 }
							}
							set_temp_variable = { gip_imr = global.building_advanced_input_resource_2@var:bld_tkn }

							set_temp_variable = { gip_exp = global.building_advanced_input_amount_2@var:bld_tkn }
							multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = price@var:gip_imr }
							multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = input_modifier_temp }
							multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = throughput_modifier_temp }
							multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = size@var:bld_tkn }
							subtract_from_temp_variable = { gip_profit = gip_exp }
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { global.building_advanced_input_amount_3@var:bld_tkn > 0 }
							}
							set_temp_variable = { gip_imr = global.building_advanced_input_resource_3@var:bld_tkn }

							set_temp_variable = { gip_exp = global.building_advanced_input_amount_3@var:bld_tkn }
							multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = price@var:gip_imr }
							multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = input_modifier_temp }
							multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = throughput_modifier_temp }
							multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = size@var:bld_tkn }
							subtract_from_temp_variable = { gip_profit = gip_exp }
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { global.building_advanced_input_amount_4@var:bld_tkn > 0 }
							}
							set_temp_variable = { gip_imr = global.building_advanced_input_resource_4@var:bld_tkn }

			defined_text = {
				name = GetBuildingIndustrializedProfit
				text = {
					trigger = {
						set_temp_variable = { bld_tkn = v }
						set_temp_variable = { bld_o1 = global.building_output_resource_1@var:bld_tkn }
						set_temp_variable = { bld_o2 = global.building_output_resource_2@var:bld_tkn }
						set_temp_variable = { bld_o3 = global.building_output_resource_3@var:bld_tkn }
						set_temp_variable = { bld_o4 = global.building_output_resource_4@var:bld_tkn }
						set_temp_variable = { bld_o5 = global.building_output_resource_5@var:bld_tkn }

						set_temp_variable = { output_modifier_temp = building_output_factor@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { output_modifier_temp = 1 }

						set_temp_variable = { throughput_modifier_temp = building_throughput_factor@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { throughput_modifier_temp = 1 }

						set_temp_variable = { input_modifier_temp = building_input_factor@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { input_modifier_temp = 1 }

						set_temp_variable = { size_modifier_temp = building_size_factor@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { size_modifier_temp = 1 }

						#Revenue
						set_temp_variable = { gip_profit = price@var:bld_o1 }

				text = {
					trigger = {
						set_temp_variable = { bld_tkn = v }
						set_temp_variable = { bld_tmp = global.building_industrialized_output_3@var:bld_tkn }
						check_variable = { bld_tmp > 0 }
					}
					localization_key = "building_pm_industrialized_production_3_tt"
				}
				text = {
					localization_key = ""
				}
			}
			defined_text = {
				name = GetBuildingIndustrializedProduction3Amount
				text = {
					trigger = {
						set_temp_variable = { bld_tkn = v }

						set_temp_variable = { output_modifier_temp = building_output_factor@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { output_modifier_temp = 1 }

						set_temp_variable = { throughput_modifier_temp = building_throughput_factor@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { throughput_modifier_temp = 1 }

						set_temp_variable = { bld_tmp = global.building_industrialized_output_3@var:bld_tkn }
						multiply_temp_variable = { bld_tmp = size@var:bld_tkn }
						multiply_temp_variable = { bld_tmp = throughput_modifier_temp }
						multiply_temp_variable = { bld_tmp = output_modifier_temp }
					}
					localization_key = "[?bld_tmp|3]"
				}
			}

						set_temp_variable = { gip_exp = global.building_mechanized_laborers_employment@var:bld_tkn }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = 2 }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = size_modifier_temp }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = base_wage@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { avg_wage_temp = gip_exp }
						
						set_temp_variable = { gip_exp = global.building_mechanized_workers_employment@var:bld_tkn }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = 5 }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = size_modifier_temp }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = base_wage@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { avg_wage_temp = gip_exp }
						
						set_temp_variable = { gip_exp = global.building_mechanized_professionals_employment@var:bld_tkn }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = 10 }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = size_modifier_temp }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = base_wage@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { avg_wage_temp = gip_exp }
						
						set_temp_variable = { gip_exp = global.building_mechanized_specialists_employment@var:bld_tkn }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = 20 }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = size_modifier_temp }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = base_wage@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { avg_wage_temp = gip_exp }
						
						set_temp_variable = { gip_exp = global.building_mechanized_aristocrats_employment@var:bld_tkn }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = 30 }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = size_modifier_temp }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = base_wage@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { avg_wage_temp = gip_exp }
						
						set_temp_variable = { gip_exp = global.building_mechanized_capitalists_employment@var:bld_tkn }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = 50 }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = size_modifier_temp }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = base_wage@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { avg_wage_temp = gip_exp }

						divide_temp_variable = { avg_wage_temp = gip_employees }
						check_variable = { avg_wage_temp < gip_profit }
					}
					localization_key = "[?gip_profit|3G]"
				}
				text = {
					trigger = {
						check_variable = { avg_wage_temp > gip_profit }
					}
					localization_key = "[?gip_profit|3R]"
				}
				text = {
					localization_key = "[?gip_profit|3Y]"

						add_to_temp_variable = { gip_profit = gip_temp }

						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_profit = throughput_modifier_temp }

						subtract_from_temp_variable = { gip_profit = gip_exp }

				name = GetBuildingMotorizedProfit
				text = {
					trigger = {
						set_temp_variable = { bld_tkn = v }
						set_temp_variable = { bld_o1 = global.building_output_resource_1@var:bld_tkn }
						set_temp_variable = { bld_o2 = global.building_output_resource_2@var:bld_tkn }
						set_temp_variable = { bld_o3 = global.building_output_resource_3@var:bld_tkn }
						set_temp_variable = { bld_o4 = global.building_output_resource_4@var:bld_tkn }
						set_temp_variable = { bld_o5 = global.building_output_resource_5@var:bld_tkn }

						set_temp_variable = { output_modifier_temp = building_output_factor@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { output_modifier_temp = 1 }

						set_temp_variable = { throughput_modifier_temp = building_throughput_factor@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { throughput_modifier_temp = 1 }

						set_temp_variable = { input_modifier_temp = building_input_factor@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { input_modifier_temp = 1 }

						set_temp_variable = { size_modifier_temp = building_size_factor@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { size_modifier_temp = 1 }

						#Revenue
						set_temp_variable = { gip_profit = price@var:bld_o1 }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_profit = global.building_motorized_output_1@var:bld_tkn }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_profit = size@var:bld_tkn }
						
						set_temp_variable = { gip_temp = price@var:bld_o2 }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_temp = global.building_motorized_output_2@var:bld_tkn }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_temp = size@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { gip_profit = gip_temp }
						
						set_temp_variable = { gip_temp = price@var:bld_o3 }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_temp = global.building_motorized_output_3@var:bld_tkn }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_temp = size@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { gip_profit = gip_temp }

						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_temp = global.building_motorized_output_industrial_capacity@var:bld_tkn }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_temp = size@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { gip_profit = gip_temp }

						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_profit = output_modifier_temp }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_profit = throughput_modifier_temp }

						#Expenses
						set_temp_variable = { gip_exp = global.building_industrial_capacity_use@var:bld_tkn }
						set_temp_variable = { cap_modifier_temp = building_industrial_capacity_use_factor@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { cap_modifier_temp = 1 }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = size@var:bld_tkn }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = cap_modifier_temp }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = input_modifier_temp }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = throughput_modifier_temp }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = price_industrial_capacity }
						subtract_from_temp_variable = { gip_profit = gip_exp }
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { global.building_motorized_input_amount_1@var:bld_tkn > 0 }
							}
							set_temp_variable = { gip_imr = global.building_motorized_input_resource_1@var:bld_tkn }

							set_temp_variable = { gip_exp = global.building_motorized_input_amount_1@var:bld_tkn }
							multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = price@var:gip_imr }
							multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = input_modifier_temp }
							multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = throughput_modifier_temp }
							multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = size@var:bld_tkn }
							subtract_from_temp_variable = { gip_profit = gip_exp }

							set_temp_variable = { gip_exp = global.building_motorized_input_amount_2@var:bld_tkn }
							multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = price@var:gip_imr }

							multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = throughput_modifier_temp }
							multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = size@var:bld_tkn }
							subtract_from_temp_variable = { gip_profit = gip_exp }

			defined_text = {
				name = GetBuildingModernizedProfit
				text = {
					trigger = {
						set_temp_variable = { bld_tkn = v }
						set_temp_variable = { bld_o1 = global.building_output_resource_1@var:bld_tkn }
						set_temp_variable = { bld_o2 = global.building_output_resource_2@var:bld_tkn }
						set_temp_variable = { bld_o3 = global.building_output_resource_3@var:bld_tkn }
						set_temp_variable = { bld_o4 = global.building_output_resource_4@var:bld_tkn }
						set_temp_variable = { bld_o5 = global.building_output_resource_5@var:bld_tkn }

						set_temp_variable = { output_modifier_temp = building_output_factor@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { output_modifier_temp = 1 }

						set_temp_variable = { throughput_modifier_temp = building_throughput_factor@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { throughput_modifier_temp = 1 }

						set_temp_variable = { input_modifier_temp = building_input_factor@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { input_modifier_temp = 1 }

						set_temp_variable = { size_modifier_temp = building_size_factor@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { size_modifier_temp = 1 }

						#Revenue
						set_temp_variable = { gip_profit = price@var:bld_o1 }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_profit = global.building_modernized_output_1@var:bld_tkn }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_profit = size@var:bld_tkn }
						
						set_temp_variable = { gip_temp = price@var:bld_o2 }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_temp = global.building_modernized_output_2@var:bld_tkn }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_temp = size@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { gip_profit = gip_temp }
						
						set_temp_variable = { gip_temp = price@var:bld_o3 }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_temp = global.building_modernized_output_3@var:bld_tkn }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_temp = size@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { gip_profit = gip_temp }

						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = 10 }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = size_modifier_temp }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = base_wage@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { avg_wage_temp = gip_exp }
						
						set_temp_variable = { gip_exp = global.building_roboticized_specialists_employment@var:bld_tkn }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = 20 }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = size_modifier_temp }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = base_wage@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { avg_wage_temp = gip_exp }
						
						set_temp_variable = { gip_exp = global.building_roboticized_aristocrats_employment@var:bld_tkn }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = 30 }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = size_modifier_temp }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = base_wage@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { avg_wage_temp = gip_exp }
						
						set_temp_variable = { gip_exp = global.building_roboticized_capitalists_employment@var:bld_tkn }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = 50 }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = size_modifier_temp }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = base_wage@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { avg_wage_temp = gip_exp }

						divide_temp_variable = { avg_wage_temp = gip_employees }
						check_variable = { avg_wage_temp < gip_profit }
					}
					localization_key = "[?gip_profit|3G]"
				}
				text = {
					trigger = {
						check_variable = { avg_wage_temp > gip_profit }
					}
					localization_key = "[?gip_profit|3R]"
				}
				text = {
					localization_key = "[?gip_profit|3Y]"
				}
			}

			defined_text = {
				name = GetBuildingComputerizedProfit
				text = {
					trigger = {
						set_temp_variable = { bld_tkn = v }
						set_temp_variable = { bld_o1 = global.building_output_resource_1@var:bld_tkn }
						set_temp_variable = { bld_o2 = global.building_output_resource_2@var:bld_tkn }
						set_temp_variable = { bld_o3 = global.building_output_resource_3@var:bld_tkn }
						set_temp_variable = { bld_o4 = global.building_output_resource_4@var:bld_tkn }
						set_temp_variable = { bld_o5 = global.building_output_resource_5@var:bld_tkn }

						set_temp_variable = { output_modifier_temp = building_output_factor@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { output_modifier_temp = 1 }

						set_temp_variable = { throughput_modifier_temp = building_throughput_factor@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { throughput_modifier_temp = 1 }

						set_temp_variable = { input_modifier_temp = building_input_factor@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { input_modifier_temp = 1 }

						set_temp_variable = { size_modifier_temp = building_size_factor@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { size_modifier_temp = 1 }

						#Revenue
						set_temp_variable = { gip_profit = price@var:bld_o1 }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_profit = global.building_computerized_output_1@var:bld_tkn }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_profit = size@var:bld_tkn }
						
						set_temp_variable = { gip_temp = price@var:bld_o2 }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_temp = global.building_computerized_output_2@var:bld_tkn }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_temp = size@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { gip_profit = gip_temp }

						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_temp = global.building_computerized_output_3@var:bld_tkn }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_temp = size@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { gip_profit = gip_temp }

						add_to_temp_variable = { gip_profit = gip_temp }

						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_profit = output_modifier_temp }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_profit = throughput_modifier_temp }

						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = throughput_modifier_temp }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = price_industrial_capacity }
						subtract_from_temp_variable = { gip_profit = gip_exp }

							limit = {
								check_variable = { global.building_computerized_input_amount_1@var:bld_tkn > 0 }

							multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = throughput_modifier_temp }
							multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = size@var:bld_tkn }

							multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = size@var:bld_tkn }

						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = cap_modifier_temp }

						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = throughput_modifier_temp }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = price_industrial_capacity }
						subtract_from_temp_variable = { gip_profit = gip_exp }

							limit = {
								check_variable = { global.building_computerized_input_amount_1@var:bld_tkn > 0 }
							}
							set_temp_variable = { gip_imr = global.building_computerized_input_resource_1@var:bld_tkn }

							set_temp_variable = { gip_exp = global.building_computerized_input_amount_1@var:bld_tkn }
							multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = price@var:gip_imr }
							multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = input_modifier_temp }
							multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = throughput_modifier_temp }
							subtract_from_temp_variable = { gip_profit = gip_exp }

			defined_text = {
				name = GetBuildingAutomatizedProfit
				text = {
					trigger = {
						set_temp_variable = { bld_tkn = v }
						set_temp_variable = { bld_o1 = global.building_output_resource_1@var:bld_tkn }
						set_temp_variable = { bld_o2 = global.building_output_resource_2@var:bld_tkn }
						set_temp_variable = { bld_o3 = global.building_output_resource_3@var:bld_tkn }
						set_temp_variable = { bld_o4 = global.building_output_resource_4@var:bld_tkn }
						set_temp_variable = { bld_o5 = global.building_output_resource_5@var:bld_tkn }

						set_temp_variable = { output_modifier_temp = building_output_factor@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { output_modifier_temp = 1 }

						set_temp_variable = { throughput_modifier_temp = building_throughput_factor@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { throughput_modifier_temp = 1 }

						set_temp_variable = { input_modifier_temp = building_input_factor@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { input_modifier_temp = 1 }

						set_temp_variable = { size_modifier_temp = building_size_factor@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { size_modifier_temp = 1 }

						#Revenue
						set_temp_variable = { gip_profit = price@var:bld_o1 }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_profit = global.building_automatized_output_1@var:bld_tkn }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_profit = size@var:bld_tkn }
						
						set_temp_variable = { gip_temp = price@var:bld_o2 }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_temp = global.building_automatized_output_2@var:bld_tkn }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_temp = size@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { gip_profit = gip_temp }
						
						set_temp_variable = { gip_temp = price@var:bld_o3 }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_temp = global.building_automatized_output_3@var:bld_tkn }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_temp = size@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { gip_profit = gip_temp }
						
						set_temp_variable = { gip_temp = price@var:bld_o4 }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_temp = global.building_automatized_output_4@var:bld_tkn }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_temp = size@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { gip_profit = gip_temp }
						
						set_temp_variable = { gip_temp = price@var:bld_o5 }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_temp = global.building_automatized_output_5@var:bld_tkn }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_temp = size@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { gip_profit = gip_temp }
						
						set_temp_variable = { gip_temp = price_industrial_capacity }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_temp = global.building_automatized_output_industrial_capacity@var:bld_tkn }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_temp = size@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { gip_profit = gip_temp }

						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_profit = output_modifier_temp }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_profit = throughput_modifier_temp }

						#Expenses

						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = 30 }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = size_modifier_temp }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = base_wage@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { avg_wage_temp = gip_exp }
						
						set_temp_variable = { gip_exp = global.building_futurized_capitalists_employment@var:bld_tkn }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = 50 }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = size_modifier_temp }
						multiply_temp_variable = { gip_exp = base_wage@var:bld_tkn }
						add_to_temp_variable = { avg_wage_temp = gip_exp }

						divide_temp_variable = { avg_wage_temp = gip_employees }
						check_variable = { avg_wage_temp < gip_profit }
					}
					localization_key = "[?gip_profit|3G]"
				}
				text = {
					trigger = {
						check_variable = { avg_wage_temp > gip_profit }
					}
					localization_key = "[?gip_profit|3R]"
				}
				text = {
					localization_key = "[?gip_profit|3Y]"
				}
			}

	#Construction Tooltip
		defined_text = {
			name = GetBuildingConstructionTooltip
			text = {
				trigger = {
					OR = {
						check_variable = { v = token:building_subsistence_farm }
						check_variable = { v = token:building_rice_paddy }
					}
				}
				localization_key = "building_cant_build_subsistence_tt"
			}
			text = {
				trigger = {
					#always = no
					NOT = { is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT }
				}
				localization_key = "building_cant_build_control_tt"
			}
			text = {
				trigger = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { v = token:building_military_industry }
						}
						NOT = { 
							free_building_slots = {
								building = arms_factory
								size > 0
								include_locked = no
							}
						}
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { v = token:building_civilian_industry }
						}
						NOT = { 
							free_building_slots = {
								building = industrial_complex
								size > 0
								include_locked = no
							}
						}
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { v = token:building_naval_industry }
						}
						NOT = { 
							free_building_slots = {
								building = dockyard
								size > 0
								include_locked = no
							}
						}
					}
					else = {
						always = no
					}
				}
				localization_key = "building_cant_build_slots_tt"
			}
			text = {
				trigger = {
					
					set_temp_variable = { pm_temp = production_method@var:v }
					if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { pm_temp = 0 }
						}
						set_temp_variable = { gcpa = global.building_basic_construction_amount@var:v }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { pm_temp = 1 }
						}
						set_temp_variable = { gcpa = global.building_advanced_construction_amount@var:v }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { pm_temp = 2 }
						}
						set_temp_variable = { gcpa = global.building_industrialized_construction_amount@var:v }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { pm_temp = 3 }
						}
						set_temp_variable = { gcpa = global.building_mechanized_construction_amount@var:v }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { pm_temp = 4 }
						}
						set_temp_variable = { gcpa = global.building_electrified_construction_amount@var:v }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { pm_temp = 5 }
						}
						set_temp_variable = { gcpa = global.building_motorized_construction_amount@var:v }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { pm_temp = 6 }
						}
						set_temp_variable = { gcpa = global.building_modernized_construction_amount@var:v }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { pm_temp = 7 }
						}
						set_temp_variable = { gcpa = global.building_roboticized_construction_amount@var:v }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { pm_temp = 8 }
						}
						set_temp_variable = { gcpa = global.building_computerized_construction_amount@var:v }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { pm_temp = 9 }
						}
						set_temp_variable = { gcpa = global.building_digitalized_construction_amount@var:v }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { pm_temp = 10 }
						}
						set_temp_variable = { gcpa = global.building_automatized_construction_amount@var:v }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { pm_temp = 11 }
						}
						set_temp_variable = { gcpa = global.building_futurized_construction_amount@var:v }
					}

					multiply_temp_variable = { gcpa = price@token:resource_industrial_goods }
					multiply_temp_variable = { gcpa = global.start_construction_cost_multiplier }
					check_variable = { gcpa > ROOT.treasury }
				}
				localization_key = "building_cant_build_treasury_tt"
			}
			text = {
				localization_key = "building_build_tt"
			}
		}

							check_variable = { pm_temp = 10 }
						}
						set_temp_variable = { gcpa = global.building_automatized_construction_speed@var:v }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { pm_temp = 11 }
						}
						set_temp_variable = { gcpa = global.building_futurized_construction_speed@var:v }
					}
				}
				localization_key = "[?gcpa|3]"
			}
		}
		defined_text = {
			name = GetBuildingConstructionPredictedMonthlyCost

					if = {

		defined_text = {
			name = GetBuildingConstructionPredictedTime
			text = {
				trigger = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { size@var:v > 0 }
						}
						set_temp_variable = { pm_temp = production_method@var:v }
					}
					else = {
						set_temp_variable = { pm_temp = controller:latest_production_method@var:v }
					}

					if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { pm_temp = 0 }
						}
						set_temp_variable = { total_amount_temp = global.building_basic_construction_amount@var:v }
						set_temp_variable = { monthly_amount_temp = global.building_basic_construction_speed@var:v }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { pm_temp = 1 }
						}
						set_temp_variable = { total_amount_temp = global.building_advanced_construction_amount@var:v }
						set_temp_variable = { monthly_amount_temp = global.building_advanced_construction_speed@var:v }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { pm_temp = 2 }
						}
						set_temp_variable = { total_amount_temp = global.building_industrialized_construction_amount@var:v }
						set_temp_variable = { monthly_amount_temp = global.building_industrialized_construction_speed@var:v }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { pm_temp = 3 }
						}
						set_temp_variable = { total_amount_temp = global.building_mechanized_construction_amount@var:v }
						set_temp_variable = { monthly_amount_temp = global.building_mechanized_construction_speed@var:v }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { pm_temp = 4 }
						}
						set_temp_variable = { total_amount_temp = global.building_electrified_construction_amount@var:v }
						set_temp_variable = { monthly_amount_temp = global.building_electrified_construction_speed@var:v }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { pm_temp = 5 }
						}
						set_temp_variable = { total_amount_temp = global.building_motorized_construction_amount@var:v }
						set_temp_variable = { monthly_amount_temp = global.building_motorized_construction_speed@var:v }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { pm_temp = 6 }
						}
						set_temp_variable = { total_amount_temp = global.building_modernized_construction_amount@var:v }
						set_temp_variable = { monthly_amount_temp = global.building_modernized_construction_speed@var:v }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { pm_temp = 7 }
						}
						set_temp_variable = { total_amount_temp = global.building_roboticized_construction_amount@var:v }
						set_temp_variable = { monthly_amount_temp = global.building_roboticized_construction_speed@var:v }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { pm_temp = 8 }
						}
						set_temp_variable = { total_amount_temp = global.building_computerized_construction_amount@var:v }
						set_temp_variable = { monthly_amount_temp = global.building_computerized_construction_speed@var:v }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { pm_temp = 9 }
						}
						set_temp_variable = { total_amount_temp = global.building_digitalized_construction_amount@var:v }
						set_temp_variable = { monthly_amount_temp = global.building_digitalized_construction_speed@var:v }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { pm_temp = 10 }
						}
						set_temp_variable = { total_amount_temp = global.building_automatized_construction_amount@var:v }
						set_temp_variable = { monthly_amount_temp = global.building_automatized_construction_speed@var:v }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { pm_temp = 11 }
						}
						set_temp_variable = { total_amount_temp = global.building_futurized_construction_amount@var:v }
						set_temp_variable = { monthly_amount_temp = global.building_futurized_construction_speed@var:v }
					}

					set_temp_variable = { months_temp = total_amount_temp }
					divide_temp_variable = { months_temp = monthly_amount_temp }
					add_to_temp_variable = { months_temp = 0.499 }
					round_temp_variable = months_temp
					
					set_temp_variable = { years_temp = months_temp }
					divide_temp_variable = { years_temp = 12 }
					subtract_from_temp_variable = { years_temp = 0.5 }
					round_temp_variable = years_temp

					set_temp_variable = { months_sub_temp = years_temp }
					multiply_temp_variable = { months_sub_temp = 12 }
					subtract_from_temp_variable = { months_temp = months_sub_temp }

					always = yes
				}
				localization_key = "building_build_time_tt"
			}
		}
		defined_text = {
			name = GetBuildingConstructionTime
			text = {
				trigger = {
					set_temp_variable = { months_temp = construction_amount@var:v }
					divide_temp_variable = { months_temp = construction_speed@var:v }
					add_to_temp_variable = { months_temp = 0.499 }
					round_temp_variable = months_temp
					
					set_temp_variable = { years_temp = months_temp }
					divide_temp_variable = { years_temp = 12 }
					subtract_from_temp_variable = { years_temp = 0.5 }
					round_temp_variable = years_temp

					set_temp_variable = { months_sub_temp = years_temp }
					multiply_temp_variable = { months_sub_temp = 12 }
					subtract_from_temp_variable = { months_temp = months_sub_temp }

					always = yes
				}
				localization_key = "building_build_time_tt"
			}
		}
		defined_text = {
			name = GetBuildingConstructionFinancer

        }

#Infrastructure
    defined_text = {
        name = GetInfrastructureCrumblingColor
        text = {
            trigger = {
                check_variable = { infrastructure_crumbling_ticks > 0 }
                check_variable = { infrastructure_industrial_goods_fulfilled_percentage < global.infrastructure_crumbling_threshold }
            }
            localization_key = red_loc
        }
        text = {
            trigger = {
                check_variable = { infrastructure_crumbling_ticks > 0 }
                NOT = { check_variable = { infrastructure_industrial_goods_fulfilled_percentage < global.infrastructure_crumbling_threshold } }
            }
            localization_key = yellow_loc
        }
    }
    defined_text = {
        name = GetInfrastructureCrumbling
        text = {
            trigger = {
                check_variable = { infrastructure_crumbling_ticks > 0 }
                check_variable = { infrastructure_industrial_goods_fulfilled_percentage < global.infrastructure_crumbling_threshold }
            }
            localization_key = infrastructure_crumbling_warning_tt
        }
        text = {
            trigger = {
                check_variable = { infrastructure_crumbling_ticks > 0 }
                NOT = { check_variable = { infrastructure_industrial_goods_fulfilled_percentage < global.infrastructure_crumbling_threshold } }
            }
            localization_key = infrastructure_restoring_warning_tt
        }
    }

		text = {
			trigger = {
				multiply_temp_variable = { amount_temp = -1 }
			}
			localization_key = "[GetSpendingColor][GetAdjustedAmount]"
		}
	}

	defined_text = { # GetTreasuryAmount
		name = GetTreasuryAmount
		text = {
			trigger = {
				check_variable = { treasury > 99999.999 }
				set_temp_variable = { invest_temp = treasury }
				divide_temp_variable = { invest_temp = 1000 }
			}
			localization_key = "[?invest_temp|0]K"
		}
		text = {
			trigger = {
				check_variable = { treasury > 9999.999 }
				set_temp_variable = { invest_temp = treasury }
				divide_temp_variable = { invest_temp = 1000 }
			}
			localization_key = "[?invest_temp|1]K"
		}
		text = {
			trigger = {
				check_variable = { treasury > 999.999 }
				set_temp_variable = { invest_temp = treasury }
				divide_temp_variable = { invest_temp = 1000 }
			}
			localization_key = "[?invest_temp|2]K"
		}
		text = {
			trigger = {
				check_variable = { treasury > 99.999 }
			}
			localization_key = "[?treasury|0]"
		}
		text = {
			trigger = {
				check_variable = { treasury > 9.999 }
			}
			localization_key = "[?treasury|1]"
		}
		text = {
			trigger = {
				check_variable = { treasury > 0.999 }
			}
			localization_key = "[?treasury|2]"
		}
		text = {
			localization_key = "[?treasury|3]"
		}
	}
	defined_text = { # GetNetBudgetAmount
		name = GetNetBudgetAmount
		text = {
			trigger = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = { net_budget > 99999.999 }
					check_variable = { net_budget < -99999.999 }
				}
				set_temp_variable = { invest_temp = net_budget }
				divide_temp_variable = { invest_temp = 1000 }
			}
			localization_key = "[?invest_temp|=0]K"
		}
		text = {
			trigger = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = { net_budget > 9999.999 }
					check_variable = { net_budget < -9999.999 }
				}
				set_temp_variable = { invest_temp = net_budget }
				divide_temp_variable = { invest_temp = 1000 }
			}
			localization_key = "[?invest_temp|=1]K"
		}
		text = {
			trigger = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = { net_budget > 999.999 }
					check_variable = { net_budget < -999.999 }
				}
				set_temp_variable = { invest_temp = net_budget }
				divide_temp_variable = { invest_temp = 1000 }
			}
			localization_key = "[?invest_temp|=2]K"
		}
		text = {
			trigger = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = { net_budget > 99.999 }
					check_variable = { net_budget < -99.999 }
				}
			}
			localization_key = "[?net_budget|=0]"
		}
		text = {
			trigger = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = { net_budget > 9.999 }
					check_variable = { net_budget < -9.999 }
				}
			}
			localization_key = "[?net_budget|=1]"
		}
		text = {
			trigger = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = { net_budget > 0.999 }

			}
			localization_key = "[?net_budget|=2]"

#National Bank
	defined_text = {
		name = GetDebtLevelColor
		text = {
			trigger = { 
				check_variable = { debt_level < 1 }
			}
			localization_key = white_loc
		}
		text = {
			trigger = { 
				check_variable = { debt_level < 20 }
			}
			localization_key = yellow_loc
		}
		text = {
			localization_key = red_loc
		}
	}
	defined_text = {
		name = GetDebtAmount
		text = {
			trigger = { 
				set_temp_variable = { debt_amount_temp = debt_level }
				divide_temp_variable = { debt_amount_temp = 2 }
				multiply_temp_variable = { debt_amount_temp = gdp_amount }
				check_variable = { debt_amount_temp < 1000 }
				check_variable = { gdp_amount < 10000 }
			}
			localization_key = "[?debt_amount_temp]"
		}
		text = {
			trigger = { 
				set_temp_variable = { debt_amount_temp = debt_level }
				divide_temp_variable = { debt_amount_temp = 1000 }
				multiply_temp_variable = { debt_amount_temp = gdp_amount }
				divide_temp_variable = { debt_amount_temp = 2 }
			}
			localization_key = "[?debt_amount_temp]K"
		}
	}
	defined_text = {
		name = GetDebtToGDPRatio
		text = {
			trigger = { 
				set_temp_variable = { debt_amount_temp = debt_level }
				divide_temp_variable = { debt_amount_temp = 24 }
			}
			localization_key = "[?debt_amount_temp|%]"
		}
	}
	defined_text = {
		name = GetMaxRepaymentAmount

				check_variable = { treasury_temp < national_debt_k }

			localization_key = "[?treasury_temp]K"
		}
		text = {

#Trade
	#Macro Section
		#GetSelectedResource
			defined_text = {
				name = GetSelectedResource
				text = {
					trigger = {
						OR = {
							is_in_array = { global.resource_token_array = selected_resource }
							is_in_array = { global.military_resource_token_array = selected_resource }
						}
					}
					localization_key = "[?selected_resource.GetTokenLocalizedKey]"
				}
				text = {
					trigger = {
						has_country_flag = new_trade_route_view_open
					}
					localization_key = "selected_resource_choose_loc"
				}
				text = {
					localization_key = "selected_resource_all_loc"
				}
			}
		#
		#GetSelectedResourceIcon
			defined_text = {
				name = GetSelectedResourceIcon
				text = {
					trigger = {
						OR = {
							is_in_array = { global.resource_token_array = selected_resource }
							is_in_array = { global.military_resource_token_array = selected_resource }
						}
					}
					localization_key = "GFX_[?selected_resource.GetTokenKey]"
				}
				text = {
					localization_key = "GFX_gdp_icon"
				}
			}
		#
		#GetSelectedResourceTrade
			defined_text = {
				name = GetSelectedResourceTrade
				text = {
					trigger = {
						NOT = {
							OR = {
								is_in_array = { global.resource_token_array = selected_resource }
								is_in_array = { global.military_resource_token_array = selected_resource }
							}
						}
					}
					localization_key = "selected_resource_choose_loc"
				}
				text = {
					trigger = {
						check_variable = { offers@var:selected_resource < 0 }
						check_variable = { offers@var:selected_resource = trade@var:selected_resource }
						set_temp_variable = { tmp = offers@var:selected_resource }
						multiply_temp_variable = { tmp = -1 }
					}
					localization_key = "net_exporting"
				}
				text = {
					trigger = {
						check_variable = { offers@var:selected_resource < 0 }
						set_temp_variable = { tmp = offers@var:selected_resource }
						multiply_temp_variable = { tmp = -1 }
						set_temp_variable = { percent_temp = trade@var:selected_resource }
						divide_temp_variable = { percent_temp = offers@var:selected_resource }
					}
					localization_key = "net_exporting_capped"
				}
				text = {
					trigger = {
						check_variable = { offers@var:selected_resource > 0 }
						check_variable = { offers@var:selected_resource = trade@var:selected_resource }
					}
					localization_key = "net_importing"
				}
				text = {
					trigger = {
						check_variable = { offers@var:selected_resource > 0 }
						set_temp_variable = { percent_temp = trade@var:selected_resource }
						divide_temp_variable = { percent_temp = offers@var:selected_resource }
					}
					localization_key = "net_importing_capped"
				}
				text = {
					localization_key = "net_no_trade"
				}
			}
			defined_text = {
				name = GetSelectedResourceTradeActual
				text = {
					trigger = {
						check_variable = { offers@var:selected_resource < 0 }
						set_temp_variable = { tmp = trade@var:selected_resource }
						multiply_temp_variable = { tmp = -1 }
					}
					localization_key = "[?tmp]"
				}
				text = {
					trigger = {
						check_variable = { offers@var:selected_resource > 0 }
					}
					localization_key = "[?trade@var:selected_resource]"
				}
				text = {
					localization_key = "net_no_trade"
				}
			}
		#
		#GetImportButton
			defined_text = {
				name = GetImportButton
				text = {
					trigger = {
						NOT = { has_country_flag = new_route_export }
						has_country_flag = new_trade_route_view_open
					}
					localization_key = "GFX_new_import_route_button_pressed"
				}
				text = {
					localization_key = "GFX_new_import_route_button"
				}
			}
		#
		#GetExportButton
			defined_text = {
				name = GetExportButton
				text = {
					trigger = {
						has_country_flag = new_route_export
						has_country_flag = new_trade_route_view_open
					}
					localization_key = "GFX_new_export_route_button_pressed"
				}
				text = {
					localization_key = "GFX_new_export_route_button"
				}
			}
		#
		#GetTradeAICheckbox
			defined_text = {
				name = GetTradeAICheckbox

			}
			text = {
				localization_key = "[?controller.GetAdjective]"
			}
		}
		defined_text = {
			name = GetMarketCapital
			text = {
				trigger = {
					has_variable = market_capital
				}
				localization_key = "[?market_capital.GetCapitalVictoryPointName]"
			}
			text = {
				localization_key = "[?capital.GetCapitalVictoryPointName]"
			}
		}
		defined_text = {
			name = GetControllerMarketCapital
			text = {
				trigger = {
					CONTROLLER = { has_variable = market_capital }
				}
				localization_key = "[?controller:market_capital.GetCapitalVictoryPointName]"
			}
			text = {
				localization_key = "[?owner:capital.GetCapitalVictoryPointName]"
			}
		}
		defined_text = {
			name = GetMarketMembershipRank
			text = {
				trigger = {
					OR = {
						NOT = { has_variable = market_leader }
						check_variable = { market_leader = ROOT }
					}
				}
				localization_key = "Leader"
			}
			text = {
				trigger = { is_subject = yes }
				localization_key = "Satellite"
			}
			text = {
				localization_key = "Member"
			}
		}
		defined_text = {
			name = GetControllerMarketMembershipRank
			text = {
				trigger = {
					CONTROLLER = {
						OR = {
							NOT = { has_variable = market_leader }
							check_variable = { market_leader = THIS }
						}
					}
				}
				localization_key = "Leader"
			}
			text = {
				trigger = { controller = { is_subject = yes } }
				localization_key = "Satellite"
			}
			text = {
				localization_key = "Member"
			}
		}
		defined_text = {
			name = GetTradeStatus
			text = {
				trigger = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							has_variable = market_leader
							ROOT = { has_variable = market_leader }
							check_variable = { market_leader = ROOT.market_leader }
						}
						check_variable = { market_leader = ROOT }
						check_variable = { ROOT:market_leader = THIS }
						has_war_together_with = ROOT
					}
				}
				localization_key = "In-Block"
			}
			text = {
				trigger = {
					set_temp_variable = { country_temp = THIS }
					ROOT = { can_trade_with = yes }
				}
				localization_key = "Accessible"
			}
			text = {
				trigger = {
					has_war_with = ROOT
				}
				localization_key = "Enemy"
			}
			text = {
				localization_key = "Not Accessible"
			}
		}
		defined_text = {
			name = GetControllerTradeStatus
			text = {
				trigger = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							CONTROLLER = { has_variable = market_leader }
							ROOT = { has_variable = market_leader }
							check_variable = { CONTROLLER:market_leader = ROOT.market_leader }
						}
						check_variable = { CONTROLLER:market_leader = ROOT.id }
						check_variable = { ROOT:market_leader = CONTROLLER.id }
						CONTROLLER = { has_war_together_with = ROOT }
					}
				}
				localization_key = "In-Block"
			}
			text = {
				trigger = {
					set_temp_variable = { country_temp = controller }
					ROOT = { can_trade_with = yes }
				}
				localization_key = "Accessible"
			}
			text = {
				trigger = {
					controller = {
						has_war_with = ROOT
					}
				}
				localization_key = "Enemy"
			}
			text = {
				localization_key = "Not Accessible"
			}
		}
	#
#

#Topbar
	defined_text = {
        name = GetMoneyAmountTopbar
		text = {
            trigger = {
                set_temp_variable = {treasury_temp = treasury}
				divide_temp_variable = {treasury_temp = 1000000}
				check_variable = {treasury > 999999.99}
            }
            localization_key = "[?treasury_temp|2]M"
        }
        text = {
            trigger = {
                set_temp_variable = {treasury_temp = treasury}
				divide_temp_variable = {treasury_temp = 1000}
				check_variable = {treasury > 999.99}
            }
            localization_key = "[?treasury_temp|2]K"
        }
        text = {
            localization_key = "[?treasury|2]"
        }
    }
